     <p>
      This is a list of programs that have been broadcast on
      <a href="/wiki/Adult_Swim" title="Adult Swim">
       Adult Swim
      </a>
      (formerly
      <a href="/wiki/Cartoon_Network" title="Cartoon Network">
       Cartoon Network
      </a>
      )'s
      <a href="/wiki/Toonami" title="Toonami">
       Toonami
      </a>
      block. Broadcast times and ranges shown are with respect to the United States'
      <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Time_Zone" title="Eastern Time Zone">
       Eastern Time Zone
      </a>
      .
     </p>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Animated_series">
       Animated series
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_programs_broadcast_by_Toonami&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Animated series">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      Cartoon Network and Adult Swim have licensed a number of animated series for broadcast on the Toonami programming blocks over the years.
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Anime">

        ]
       </span>
      </span>

     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Giant_Robot_Week">
       Giant Robot Week
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_programs_broadcast_by_Toonami&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Giant Robot Week">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <p>
      From February 2428, 2003, Toonami broadcast
      <a href="/wiki/Mecha" title="Mecha">
       mecha
      </a>
      shows that were licensed by
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ADV_Films" title="ADV Films">
       ADV Films
      </a>
      , some of which were picked up by
      <a href="/wiki/Adult_Swim" title="Adult Swim">
       Adult Swim
      </a>
      . Besides
      <i>
       Robotech
      </i>
      , the following shows were featured:
     </p>
     <table class="wikitable">
      <tr>
       <th>
        Title
       </th>
       <th>
        Airdate
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-after_midnight_5-5">
         <a href="#cite_note-after_midnight-5">
          <span>
           [
          </span>
          note 1
          <span>
           ]
          </span>
         </a>
        </sup>
       </th>
       <th>
        Notes
       </th>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Dai-Guard" title="Dai-Guard">
          Dai-Guard
         </a>
        </i>
       </td>
       <td>
        February 2728, 2003
       </td>
       <td>
        Episodes 1 and 2 aired on
        <a href="/wiki/Toonami" title="Toonami">
         Toonami
        </a>
        . Has not aired since GRW.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Gigantor" title="Gigantor">
          Gigantor
         </a>
        </i>
       </td>
       <td>
        February 2428, 2003
        <br/>
        April 1, 2012
       </td>
       <td>
        <i>
         Gigantor
        </i>
        was picked up by
        <a href="/wiki/Adult_Swim" title="Adult Swim">
         Adult Swim
        </a>
        .
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Programs_featured_by_block">
       Programs featured by block
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_programs_broadcast_by_Toonami&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Programs featured by block">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      A list of the lineups and programs featured in Toonami blocks. The schedule occasionally features "Toonami In Flight" blocks which contain movies or special presentations, as well as marathons and other scheduled programming that would occupy some of Cartoon Network and Adult Swim's regular programming.
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Weekday_Toonami_on_Cartoon_Network">
       Weekday Toonami on Cartoon Network
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>

        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <h4>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Weekday_Toonami_.281997.E2.80.932004.29">
       Weekday Toonami (19972004)
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_programs_broadcast_by_Toonami&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Weekday Toonami (19972004)">

       </span>
      </span>
     </h4>
     <h5>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Moltar.27s_block_.281997.E2.80.9399.29">
       Moltar's block (199799)
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_programs_broadcast_by_Toonami&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Moltar's block (199799)">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h5>
     <p>
      Moltar from
      <i>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Space_Ghost:_Coast_to_Coast" title="Space Ghost: Coast to Coast">
        Space Ghost: Coast to Coast
       </a>
      </i>
      was the original host of Toonami, which ran on Cartoon Network from 46 PM weekdays from
      <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;speak:none">
       000000001997-03-17-0000
      </span>
      <span style="white-space:nowrap">
       March 17, 1997
      </span>
      to
      <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;speak:none">
       000000001999-09-24-0000
      </span>
      <span style="white-space:nowrap">
       September 24, 1999
      </span>
      . Programs included:
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Beast_Wars:_Transformers" title="Beast Wars: Transformers">
         Beast Wars: Transformers
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        Cartoon Roulette
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Ball_Z" title="Dragon Ball Z">
         Dragon Ball Z
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/The_Real_Adventures_of_Jonny_Quest" title="The Real Adventures of Jonny Quest">
         The Real Adventures of Jonny Quest
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/ReBoot" title="ReBoot">
         ReBoot
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Robotech_(TV_series)" title="Robotech (TV series)">
         Robotech
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sailor_Moon_(English_adaptations)" title="Sailor Moon (English adaptations)">
         Sailor Moon
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Superfriends" title="Superfriends">
         Superfriends
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Thundercats" title="Thundercats">
         Thundercats
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Voltron" title="Voltron">
         Voltron
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h5>

       TOM's blocks (19992004)
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [

     <p>
      TOM took over Toonami's hosting duties starting
      <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;speak:none">

      </span>
      <span style="white-space:nowrap">
       July 11, 1999
      </span>
      . Toonami went from a 46 PM schedule to a 47 PM schedule starting
      <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;speak:none">

      </span>
      <span style="white-space:nowrap">
       July 3, 2000
      </span>

     <h4>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Midnight_Run_.282000.E2.80.932003.29">
       Midnight Run (20002003)
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_programs_broadcast_by_Toonami&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Midnight Run (20002003)">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h4>
     <p>
      Midnight runs were moved to Weeknights at midnight, starting with Monday night/Tuesday morning to Friday night/Saturday morning. Toonami Midnight Run ran form
      <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;speak:none">
       000000002000-03-07-0000
      </span>
      <span style="white-space:nowrap">
       March 7, 2000
      </span>
      to
      <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;speak:none">
       000000002003-01-09-0000
      </span>
      <span style="white-space:nowrap">
       January 9, 2003
      </span>
      from 121 AM and included:
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/The_Big_O" title="The Big O">
         The Big O
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Ball" title="Dragon Ball">
         Dragon Ball
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Ball_Z" title="Dragon Ball Z">
         Dragon Ball Z
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/G.I._Joe:_A_Real_American_Hero_(1985_TV_series)" title="G.I. Joe: A Real American Hero (1985 TV series)">
         G.I. Joe: A Real American Hero (1985 TV series)
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gundam_0080" title="Gundam 0080">
         Gundam 0080
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gundam_Wing" title="Gundam Wing">
         Gundam Wing
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Mobile_Suit_Gundam:_The_08th_MS_Team" title="Mobile Suit Gundam: The 08th MS Team">
         Mobile Suit Gundam: The 08th MS Team
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Outlaw_Star" title="Outlaw Star">
         Outlaw Star
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tenchi_Muyo" title="Tenchi Muyo">
         Tenchi Muyo
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>

      <span class="mw-headline" id="Weekend_Toonami_on_Cartoon_Network">

      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>

     </h3>
     <h4>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Saturday_Toonami_.281997.E2.80.9399.29">
       Saturday Toonami (199799)
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_programs_broadcast_by_Toonami&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Saturday Toonami (199799)">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h4>
     <p>
      Saturday Toonami ran from
      <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;speak:none">
       000000001997-07-05-0000
      </span>
      <span style="white-space:nowrap">
       July 5, 1997
      </span>
      to
      <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;speak:none">
       000000001998-10-03-0000
      </span>
      <span style="white-space:nowrap">
       October 3, 1998
      </span>
      at 79 PM and included the following programs:
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <i>
        Cartoon Roulette
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/The_Real_Adventures_of_Jonny_Quest" title="The Real Adventures of Jonny Quest">
         The Real Adventures of Jonny Quest
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Robotech_(TV_series)" title="Robotech (TV series)">
         Robotech
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Thundercats" title="Thundercats">
         Thundercats
        </a>
       </i>

     <h4>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Midnight_Run_.281999.E2.80.932000.29">
       Midnight Run (19992000)
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_programs_broadcast_by_Toonami&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Midnight Run (19992000)">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h4>
     <p>
      Toonami's Midnight Run programming block started on Sunday at midnight and ran from 125 AM. It ran from
      <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;speak:none">
       000000001999-07-11-0000
      </span>
      <span style="white-space:nowrap">
       July 11, 1999
      </span>
      to
      <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;speak:none">
       000000002000-03-05-0000
      </span>
      <span style="white-space:nowrap">
       March 5, 2000
      </span>
      , after which it was moved to a weeknight Midnight Run. It included the following programs:
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <i>
        Cartoon Roulette
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Ball_Z" title="Dragon Ball Z">
         Dragon Ball Z
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/G-Force:_Guardians_of_Space" title="G-Force: Guardians of Space">
         G-Force: Guardians of Space
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/The_Powerpuff_Girls" title="The Powerpuff Girls">
         The Powerpuff Girls
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/The_Real_Adventures_of_Jonny_Quest" title="The Real Adventures of Jonny Quest">
         The Real Adventures of Jonny Quest
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/ReBoot" title="ReBoot">
         ReBoot
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Robotech_(TV_series)" title="Robotech (TV series)">
         Robotech
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Ronin_Warriors" title="Ronin Warriors">
         Ronin Warriors
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sailor_Moon_(English_adaptations)" title="Sailor Moon (English adaptations)">
         Sailor Moon
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Thundercats" title="Thundercats">
         Thundercats
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Voltron" title="Voltron">
         Voltron
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h4>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Rising_Sun_.282000.E2.80.9301.29">
       Rising Sun (200001)
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_programs_broadcast_by_Toonami&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Rising Sun (200001)">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h4>
     <p>
      Toonami's Rising Sun programming block ran on Saturday mornings from
      <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;speak:none">
       000000002000-04-15-0000
      </span>
      <span style="white-space:nowrap">
       April 15, 2000
      </span>
      to
      <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;speak:none">
       000000002001-03-03-0000
      </span>
      <span style="white-space:nowrap">
       March 3, 2001
      </span>
      from 9 AM 12 PM from April 15  September 2, 10 AM 1 PM from September 9  December 9, 2000, and 11 AM 1 PM from December 16, 2000  March 3, 2001 . It included the following programs:
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Batman:_The_Animated_Series" title="Batman: The Animated Series">
         Batman: The Animated Series
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Ball_Z" title="Dragon Ball Z">
         Dragon Ball Z
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gundam_Wing" title="Gundam Wing">
         Gundam Wing
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/The_Powerpuff_Girls" title="The Powerpuff Girls">
         The Powerpuff Girls
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Ronin_Warriors" title="Ronin Warriors">
         Ronin Warriors
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Tenchi_Muyo!" title="Tenchi Muyo!">
         Tenchi Muyo!
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Thundercats" title="Thundercats">
         Thundercats
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sailor_Moon_(English_adaptations)" title="Sailor Moon (English adaptations)">
         Sailor Moon
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h4>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Super_Saturday_.282001.E2.80.9303.29">
       Super Saturday (200103)
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_programs_broadcast_by_Toonami&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Super Saturday (200103)">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h4>
     <p>
      Toonami's Saturday afternoon programming block ran from October 2001 to March 2003 from 13 PM, later changing to 14 PM in March 2002. It included the following programs:
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Ball" title="Dragon Ball">
         Dragon Ball
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Ball_Z" title="Dragon Ball Z">
         Dragon Ball Z
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/G-Gundam" title="G-Gundam">
         G-Gundam
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/.hack//SIGN" title=".hack//SIGN">
         .hack//SIGN
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/He-Man_and_the_Masters_of_the_Universe_(2002_TV_series)" title="He-Man and the Masters of the Universe (2002 TV series)">
         He-Man and the Masters of the Universe (2002 TV series)
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Samurai_Jack" title="Samurai Jack">
         Samurai Jack
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Transformers:_Armada" title="Transformers: Armada">
         Transformers: Armada
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Zoids:_Chaotic_Century" title="Zoids: Chaotic Century">
         Zoids: Chaotic Century
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h4>

      <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;speak:none">

      </span>

     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Toonami_lineups_on_Adult_Swim_.282012.E2.80.93present.29">

       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">

      <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;speak:none">

       May 27, 2012

     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Toonami_special_blocks">
       Toonami special blocks
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_programs_broadcast_by_Toonami&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Toonami special blocks">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <p>
      Some of the special blocks that have aired in Toonami during its run on Cartoon Network:
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       Toonami Lunar Eclipse (1999):
       <i>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sailor_Moon_(English_adaptations)" title="Sailor Moon (English adaptations)">
         Sailor Moon
        </a>
       </i>
       marathon
      </li>
      <li>
       Toonami DBZ20XL (1999): a week of
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Ball_Z" title="Dragon Ball Z">
         Dragon Ball Z
        </a>
       </i>
       episodes during Weekday Toonami
      </li>
      <li>
       Toonami DBZ20XL Movie Marathon (1999):
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Ball_Z:_The_Tree_of_Might" title="Dragon Ball Z: The Tree of Might">
         Dragon Ball Z: The Tree of Might
        </a>
       </i>
       ,
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Ball_Z:_The_World%27s_Strongest" title="Dragon Ball Z: The World's Strongest">
         Dragon Ball Z: The World's Strongest
        </a>
       </i>
       ,
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Ball_Z:_Dead_Zone" title="Dragon Ball Z: Dead Zone">
         Dragon Ball Z: Dead Zone
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       DBZ President's Day Movie Marathon (2000):
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Ball_Z:_The_Tree_of_Might" title="Dragon Ball Z: The Tree of Might">
         Dragon Ball Z: The Tree of Might
        </a>
       </i>
       ,
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Ball_Z:_The_World%27s_Strongest" title="Dragon Ball Z: The World's Strongest">
         Dragon Ball Z: The World's Strongest
        </a>
       </i>
       ,
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Ball_Z:_Dead_Zone" title="Dragon Ball Z: Dead Zone">
         Dragon Ball Z: Dead Zone
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       New Year's Eve-il (2000,2001):
       <i>
        Dragon Ball Z
       </i>
       episodes
      </li>
      <li>
       Zoids Cubed (2001):
       <i>
        Zoids: New Century Zero
       </i>
       episodes
      </li>
      <li>
       Batman VS Superman (2002): alternating episodes from
       <i>
        Batman: The Animated Series
       </i>
       and
       <i>
        Superman: The Animated Series
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       April Fools Joker Virus (2002): episodes from
       <i>
        Batman: The Animated Series
       </i>
       featuring
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Joker" title="The Joker">
        The Joker
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       Naruto Years Eve (New Year's Eve 2005):
       <i>
        Naruto
       </i>
       marathon
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="#Giant_Robot_Week">
        Giant Robot Week
       </a>
       (February 2428, 2003)
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Toonami#April_Fools.27_Day_2012" title="Toonami">
        April Fools (2012)
       </a>
       : a run of Toonami-related shows on Adult Swim
      </li>
     </ul>
